<style type="text/css">
#player-big, #cinema-off, #cinema-div, #embed-div, #related-div { display: none; }
#cinema-off { z-index: 9998; position: relative; }
#player_code { margin: 0 auto; z-index: 9998; position: relative; }

<script type="text/javascript">

function stretch_overlay() {
	$( '#cinema-div' ).height( $(document).height() );
}

makeBigPlayer = function() {
	$('#player_code object').attr( 'width', $('#player_code object').attr('width') * 2 );
	$('#player_code object').attr( 'height', $('#player_code object').attr('height') * 2 );
	$('#vid_img').height( $('#player_code object').attr('height') );
	$('#vid_img').width( $('#player_code object').attr('width') );
	$('#player_code').width( $('#player_code object').attr('width') );
	$('#player_code').css( 'top', 0 );
};
makeSmallPlayer = function() {
	$('#player_code object').attr( 'width', $('#player_code object').attr('width') / 2 );
	$('#player_code object').attr( 'height', $('#player_code object').attr('height') / 2 );
	$('#vid_img').height( $('#player_code object').attr('height') );
	$('#vid_img').width( $('#player_code object').attr('width') );
	$('#player_code').width( $('#player_code object').attr('width') );
	$('#player_code').css( 'top', $('#player_code object').attr('height') / 2 );
};

$(document).ready(function() {
	$("#player-big-but").click( function() {
		makeBigPlayer();
		$("#player-small").show();
		$("#player-big").hide();
		return false;
	});

	$("#player-small-but").click( function() {
		makeSmallPlayer();
		$("#player-big").show();
		$("#player-small").hide();
		return false;
	});

	$("#embed-but").click( function() {
		if ($('#embed-div').is(':visible')) {
			$('#embed-div').hide();
		} else {
			$("#embed-div").show();
		}
		return false;
	});

	$("#related-but").click( function() {
		$("#related-div").show();
		return false;
	});

	$("#cinema-on-but").click( function() {
		stretch_overlay();
		$("#cinema-div").show();
		$('#cinema-on').hide();
		$('#cinema-off').show();
		return false;
	});

	$("#cinema-off-but").click( function() {
		$("#cinema-div").hide();
		$('#cinema-off').hide();
		$('#cinema-on').show();
		return false;
	});
	
	if ( $('#player_code object').length ) {
		$('#player_code object').attr('width', parseInt($('#player_code').css('width')));
		$('#player_code object').attr('height', parseInt($('#player_code').css('height'))-20);
		$('#player_code').css('text-align', 'left');
	}
});
</script>
<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
    var init_w = 960;
    var init_h = 480;
    var curr_w = init_w;
    var curr_h = init_h;
    //
    var w_ar   = init_h / init_w; // multiply with WIDTH when it's changed.
    var h_ar   = init_w / init_h; // multiply with HEIGHT when it's changed.
    //
    $(document).ready(function(){
	$('#vw').change(function(){
	    prev_h = curr_h; prev_w = curr_w;
	    curr_w = parseInt(this.value);
	    if (curr_w == 'undefined' || curr_w == '') {
		this.value = init_w;
		curr_w = init_w;
	    } else {
		this.value = curr_w;
	    }
	    if ($('#kar').is(':checked'))
		curr_h = parseInt(curr_w * w_ar);
	    $('#vh').val(curr_h);
	    applySize();
	});
	//
	$('#vh').change(function(){
	    prev_h = curr_h; prev_w = curr_w;
	    curr_h = parseInt(this.value);
	    if (curr_h == 'undefined' || curr_h == '') {
		this.value = init_h;
		curr_h = init_h;
	    } else {
		this.value = curr_h;
	    }
	    if ($('#kar').is(':checked'))
		curr_w = parseInt(curr_h * h_ar);
	    $('#vw').val(curr_w);
	    applySize();
	});
	//
	$('#cusSelect1Options li').click(function(){
    	    order = this.id.replace('cusSelect1Option','')*1;
	    el = $('#vso'+order);
	    prev_h = curr_h; prev_w = curr_w;
	    curr_h = parseInt(init_h * el.val());
	    curr_w = parseInt(init_w * el.val());
	    $('#vw').val(curr_w);
	    $('#vh').val(curr_h);				    
	    applySize();
	});
	applySize = function() {
	    $('#ic4-4932857').html($('#ic4-4932857').html().replace('WIDTH='+prev_w,'WIDTH='+curr_w).replace('HEIGHT='+prev_h,'HEIGHT='+curr_h).replace('width=\''+prev_w, 'width=\''+curr_w).replace('height=\''+prev_h,'height=\''+curr_h).replace(prev_w+'x'+prev_h,curr_w+'x'+curr_h));
	    $('#ic5-4932857').html($('#ic5-4932857').html().replace('WIDTH='+prev_w,'WIDTH='+curr_w).replace('HEIGHT='+prev_h,'HEIGHT='+curr_h).replace('width=\''+prev_w, 'width=\''+curr_w).replace('height=\''+prev_h,'height=\''+curr_h).replace(prev_w+'x'+prev_h,curr_w+'x'+curr_h));
	};
    });
</script>

{

}
